###########################
# Adolf Hitler appointed as chancellor
###########################
news_event = {
	id = GER_Reichskanzler_Hitler.6
	title = {
		text = GER_Reichskanzler_Hitler.6.t
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
			}
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = GER_Reichskanzler_Hitler.6.t.GER
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GER_Reichskanzler_Hitler.6.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GER_Reichskanzler_Hitler.6.d.GER
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Adolf_Hitler_Appointed_Chancellor
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Hopefully that doesn't go wrong...
	option = {
		name = GER_Reichskanzler_Hitler.6.A
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
			}
		}
	}
	# Don't forget how people laughed at me 15 years ago
	option = {
		name = GER_Reichskanzler_Hitler.6.B
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		remove_ideas = {
			GER_A_State_Within_a_State
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = {
				GER_Kurt_von_Schleicher_HoG
				GER_Franz_Bracht_MoS
			}
		}
		add_ideas = {
			GER_Adolf_Hitler_HoG
			GER_Wilhelm_Frick_MoS
		}
		# Populate array with factions
		clear_array = active_factions_array
		set_temp_variable = {
			faction_id = 16
		}		#SA
		add_active_faction = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			faction_id = 17
		}		#SS
		add_active_faction = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			faction_id = 18
		}		#Reichswehr
		add_active_faction = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			faction_id = 29
		}
		add_active_faction = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			faction_id = 30
		}
		add_active_faction = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			faction_id = 31
		}
		add_active_faction = yes
		# Set faction influence
		set_variable = {
			faction_influence_18 = 100
		}
		# Set random loyalty and influence values
		set_variable = {
			faction_loyalty_18 = random
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			faction_loyalty_18 = 100
		}
		# Add correct faction ideas
		set_temp_variable = {
			faction_id = 18
		}
		add_faction_idea = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				faction_id = 18
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				influence_to_add = -90
			}
			change_faction_influence = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				faction_id = 17
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				influence_to_add = -5
			}
			change_faction_influence = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				faction_id = 16
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				loyalty_to_add = 50
			}
			change_faction_loyalty = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				faction_id = 17
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				loyalty_to_add = 80
			}
			change_faction_loyalty = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				faction_id = 29
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				loyalty_to_add = 80
			}
			change_faction_loyalty = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				faction_id = 30
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				loyalty_to_add = 10
			}
			change_faction_loyalty = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				faction_id = 31
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				loyalty_to_add = 50
			}
			change_faction_loyalty = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				party_id = 1
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				support_to_add = 1
			}
			change_party_support = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				party_id = 3
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				support_to_add = -0.3
			}
			change_party_support = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				party_id = 4
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				support_to_add = -1
			}
			change_party_support = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				party_id = 7
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				support_to_add = -1
			}
			change_party_support = yes
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian
				long_name = GER_authoritarian_party_NSDAP_long
				name = GER_authoritarian_party_NSDAP
			}
			news_event = {
				id = GER_Reichskanzler_Hitler.7
				days = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

# German Federal Election, March 1933
###########################
country_event = {
	id = GER_Machtergreifung.1
	title = GER_Machtergreifung.1.t
	desc = GER_Machtergreifung.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_GER_1933_Elections
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
		date > 1933.1.1
		has_start_date < 1936.01.01
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian
				election_frequency = 48
			}
		}
	}
	# NSDAP Victory
	option = {
		name = GER_Machtergreifung.1.A
		set_country_flag = GER_1933_NSDAP_Victory
		set_parliament_parties_influence = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			party_id = 3
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			support_to_add = 1
		}
		change_party_support = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			party_id = 4
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			support_to_add = -1
		}
		change_party_support = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			party_id = 7
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			support_to_add = -1
		}
		change_party_support = yes
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = GER_Book_Burnings.1
	title = GER_Book_Burnings.1.t
	desc = GER_Book_Burnings.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Animated_Book_burning
	#picture = GFX_news_GER_Nazi_Book_Burning
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			scoped_sound_effect = "GER_Book_Burning_Soundeffect"
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		date > 1933.5.10
		has_start_date < 1933.5.10
	}
	# Feed the flames!
	option = {
		name = GER_Book_Burnings.1.A
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		add_stability = -0.025
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = GER_Book_Burnings.2
				days = 124
			}
		}
	}
	# These flames have only made Europe a darker place
	option = {
		name = GER_Book_Burnings.1.B
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
			}
		}
	}
}

###########################
# Pass the Enabling Act
###########################
news_event = {
	id = GER_Enabling_Act.3
	title = GER_Enabling_Act.3.t
	desc = {
		text = GER_Enabling_Act.3.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GER_Enabling_Act.3.d.GER
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Enabling_Act
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_start_date < 1936.1.1
	}
	# There is no room for opposition!!
	option = {
		name = GER_Enabling_Act.3.A
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_Enabling_Act.3.A.tt
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascist
		}
		add_ideas = GER_Paul_Von_Hindenburg_HoG
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_The_Weimar_Era
			add_idea = GER_Limits_of_the_Weimar_Institutions
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = authoritarian
			long_name = GER_authoritarian_party_DNVP_long
			name = GER_authoritarian_party_DNVP
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_Enabling_Act
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = GER_Adolf_Hitler_HoG
			dissolve_parliament = yes
		}
	}
	# And this is how democracy dies... with thunderous applause. (World)
	option = {
		name = GER_Enabling_Act.3.B
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = GER_Stahlpakt.1
	title = GER_Stahlpakt.1.t
	desc = GER_Stahlpakt.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_GER_Rome_Berlin_Axis
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#Join
	option = {
		name = GER_Stahlpakt.1.A
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
		news_event = {
			id = GER_Stahlpakt.2
			hours = 12
		}
	}
	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = GER_Stahlpakt.1.B
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				factor = 50
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = GER_Stahlpakt.3
				hours = 12
			}
		}
	}
}
###########################
#  Germany and Italy form a Stahlpakt
###########################
news_event = {
	id = GER_Stahlpakt.2
	title = GER_Stahlpakt.2.t
	desc = GER_Stahlpakt.2.d
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Stahlpakt
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				create_faction = FACTION_Axis_Powers
				add_to_faction = ITA
			}
		}
	}
	# We shall finally achieve greatness!
	option = {
		name = GER_Stahlpakt.2.A
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = GER
				original_tag = ITA
			}
		}
	}
	# Another interesting development...
	option = {
		name = GER_Stahlpakt.2.A
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = GER
					original_tag = ITA
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#  Hitler issues an Ultimatum!
###########################
country_event = {
	id = GER_Anschluss.5
	title = GER_Anschluss.5.t
	desc = GER_Anschluss.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_GER_German_Infantry_1936
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Accept
	option = {
		name = GER_Anschluss.5.A
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				GER = {
					has_army_size = {
						size < 40
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				GER = {
					has_army_size = {
						size > 39
					}
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			news_event = {
				hours = 2
				id = GER_Anschluss.6
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
	}
	# Refuse
	option = {
		name = GER_Anschluss.5.B
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				GER = {
					has_army_size = {
						size > 39
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				GER = {
					has_army_size = {
						size < 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = GER_anschluss_rejected
			}
			country_event = {
				id = GER_Anschluss.7
				hours = 2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
				}
				remove_from_faction = AUS
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = GER_Anschluss.6
	title = GER_Anschluss.6.t
	desc = GER_Anschluss.6.d
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Anschluss
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#Finally!
	option = {
		name = GER_Anschluss.6.A
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		add_named_threat = {
			threat = 5
			name = GER_Anschluss.6
		}
		AUS = {
			remove_state_claim = 39
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = AUS
			transfer_troops = no
		}
		add_state_claim = 69
		add_state_claim = 74
		add_state_claim = 1105
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = GER_AUS_Anschluss
			GER = {
				set_country_flag = AUS_annexed
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = GER_Anschluss.6.B
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = GER_Anschluss.7.d

			type = annex_everything
			target = AUS
		}
	}

# OKL Reorganization

country_event = {
	id = GER_Luftwaffe.1
	title = GER_Luftwaffe.1.t
	desc = GER_Luftwaffe.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_GER_Hermann_Goering_1938
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#Udet is fit for the Job (CAS)
	option = {
		name = GER_Luftwaffe.1.A
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_tech = formation_flying
					has_tech = force_rotation
					has_tech = air_superiority
				}
			}
			set_technology = {
				formation_flying = 1
			}
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			uses = 2
			bonus = 0.1
			category = cas_bomber
		}
		air_experience = 50
		add_political_power = -50
	}
	#Keep Milch in Officer (Fighters)
	option = {
		name = GER_Luftwaffe.1.B
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_tech = formation_flying
					has_tech = force_rotation
					has_tech = air_superiority
				}
			}
			set_technology = {
				formation_flying = 1
			}
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			uses = 2
			bonus = 0.07
			category = light_fighter
		}
		air_experience = 5
		add_political_power = 10
	}
	#Resume Wever's Plan (Strategic Bombers)
	option = {
		name = GER_Luftwaffe.1.C
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_tech = formation_flying
					has_tech = force_rotation
					has_tech = air_superiority
				}
			}
			set_technology = {
				air_superiority = 1
			}
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			uses = 1
			bonus = 0.2
			category = cat_strategic_bomber
		}
	}
}

	title = GER_BlombergFristschAffair.3.t
	desc = GER_BlombergFristschAffair.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_GER_Hitler_and_Wehrmacht_Generals
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Ser Gut
	option = {
		name = GER_BlombergFristschAffair.3.A
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_Werner_von_Blomberg_CoStaff
			}
			remove_ideas = GER_Werner_von_Blomberg_CoStaff
			add_ideas = GER_Wilhelm_Keitel_CoStaff
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_Ludwig_Beck_CoArmy
			}
			remove_ideas = GER_Ludwig_Beck_CoArmy
			add_ideas = GER_Franz_Halder_CoArmy
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_Great_General_Staff
			add_idea = GER_Great_General_Staff_OKW
		}
	}
}
###########################
# General Andrey Vlasov captured
###########################
country_event = {
	id = GER_Ostfront.1
	title = GER_Ostfront.1.t
	desc = GER_Ostfront.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_GER_Andrey_Vlasov_Captured
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#Put him to work
	option = {
		name = GER_Ostfront.1.A
		add_political_power = -50
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = { has_character = SOV_Andrey_Vlasov }
			random_character = {
				limit = { is_character = SOV_Andrey_Vlasov }
				set_nationality = GER
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = Germany.34_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GER_ROA_deployed
			load_oob = GER_ROA
		}
	}
	#Keep him in chains
	option = {
		name = GER_Ostfront.1.B
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}
}

	desc = GER_Olympics.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_GER_1936_Olympics
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes
	# Let the games begin!
	option = {
		name = GER_Olympics.1.A
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				days = 15
				id = GER_Olympics.2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = GER_Olympics.1.A
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = GER_AustrianPutsch.1
	title = GER_AustrianPutsch.1.t
	desc = GER_AustrianPutsch.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Hans_Frank
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes	#8 March '33
	major = yes
	show_major = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = AUS
			original_tag = GER
		}
	}
	# He has a point, we must protect our brethren
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.1.A
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_AustrianPutsch.1.A.tt
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = protest_action_light
		}
	}
	# He has a point, we must protect our brethren
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.1.B
		trigger = {
			original_tag = AUS
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}
}

	id = GER_AustrianPutsch.2
	title = GER_AustrianPutsch.2.t
	desc = GER_AustrianPutsch.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_AUS_Austrian_Army
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# We must organize a move from Bavaria
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.2.A
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_AustrianPutsch.2.A.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = GER_Stage_Coup_in_Austria
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -150
		}
		AUS = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = AUS_German_Boycott
				days = 1120				#Austro-German Agreement
			}
		}
	}
	# This is not worth our time
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.2.B
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}
#########################################################################
# The July Putsch Fails! (Austria)
#########################################################################
news_event = {
	id = GER_AustrianPutsch.3
	title = GER_AustrianPutsch.3.t
	desc = {
		text = GER_AustrianPutsch.3.d.AUS
		trigger = {
			original_tag = AUS
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GER_AustrianPutsch.3.d.GER
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GER_AustrianPutsch.3.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
				original_tag = AUS
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_news_AUS_July_Putsch_2
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			AUS = {
				kill_country_leader = yes
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Kurt Schuschnigg"
					desc = ""
					picture = GFX_P_F_Kurt_Schuschnigg
					ideology = clerical_fascism
					traits = {
						POSITION_Chancellor
						SUBIDEOLOGY_Clerical_Fascism
						L_Silent_Workhorse
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# The Nazis will pay for this!
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.3.A
		trigger = {
			original_tag = AUS
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
	}
	# Ignore the development
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.3.B
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_political_power = -50
	}
	# We must save our brothers and invade!
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.3.C
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_war_support = 0.1
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_AustrianPutsch.3.C.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = AUS
				type = annex_everything
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AUS
				}
				add_core_of = GER
			}
			news_event = {
				id = GER_AustrianPutsch.5
				hours = 12
			}
		}
	}
	# Ignore the development
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.3.D
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
				original_tag = AUS
			}
		}
	}
}
#########################################################################
# The July Putsch Succeeds (Austria)
#########################################################################
news_event = {
	id = GER_AustrianPutsch.4
	title = GER_AustrianPutsch.4.t
	desc = {
		text = GER_AustrianPutsch.4.d.AUS
		trigger = {
			original_tag = AUS
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GER_AustrianPutsch.4.d.GER
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GER_AustrianPutsch.4.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
				original_tag = AUS
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Anschluss
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# The rebirth of the Osterreich
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.4.A
		trigger = {
			original_tag = AUS
		}
		add_stability = -0.15
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = fascist
			long_name = AUS_fascist_party_long
			name = AUS_fascist_party
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Anton Rintelen"
			desc = ""
			picture = GFX_P_F_Anton_Rintelen
			ideology = national_socialism
			traits = {
				POSITION_Chancellor
				SUBIDEOLOGY_National_Socialism
				L_Happy_Amateur
			}
		}
	}
	# Excellent! We must assume our political control immediately!
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.4.B
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		set_autonomy = {
			target = AUS
			autonomy_state = AUTONOMY_Reichskommissariat
		}
		AUS = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_GER
		}
	}
	# Excellent! We must assume our political control immediately!
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.4.C
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
				original_tag = AUS
			}
		}
	}
}
#########################################################################
# Germany Invades Austria
#########################################################################
news_event = {
	id = GER_AustrianPutsch.5
	title = GER_AustrianPutsch.5.t
	desc = GER_AustrianPutsch.5.d
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Dutch_Border
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.5.A
		trigger = {
			original_tag = AUS
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}
	#
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.5.B
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		add_war_support = 0.1
		set_global_flag = GER_Brother_War
	}
	#
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.5.C
		trigger = {
			original_tag = ITA
		}
		add_to_war = {
			targeted_alliance = AUS
			enemy = GER
			hostility_reason = asked_to_join
		}
		AUS = {
			give_military_access = ITA
		}
		news_event = {
			id = GER_AustrianPutsch.6
			hours = 12
		}
	}
	# How can the Austrians hope to win?
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.5.D
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
				original_tag = AUS
				has_government = communist
			}
		}
	}
	# How can the Austrians hope to win?
	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.5.E
		trigger = {
			has_government = communist
		}
	}
}

#########################################################################
# Italy wins the brother war
#########################################################################
country_event = {
	id = GER_AustrianPutsch.7
	title = GER_AustrianPutsch.7.t
	desc = GER_AustrianPutsch.7.d
	picture = GFX_news_ITA_Italian_Soldiers
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_global_flag = GER_Brother_War
		any_country = {
			OR = {
				tag = ITA
				is_subject_of = ITA
				tag = AUS
				is_subject_of = AUS
			}
			controls_state = 52 #Bavaria
			controls_state = 53 #Bavaria
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = GER_AustrianPutsch.7.A
		white_peace = ITA
		white_peace = AUS
		clr_global_flag = GER_Brother_War
		add_stability = -0.3
		add_war_support = -0.4
	}
}

			limit = {
				has_country_flag = Berlin_Pact_Member
			}
			give_guarantee = GER
			if = {
				limit = {
					ITA = {
						has_country_flag = Berlin_Pact_Member
					}
				}
				give_guarantee = ITA
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					JAP = {
						has_country_flag = Berlin_Pact_Member
					}
				}
				give_guarantee = JAP
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = GER_Berlin_Pact.4
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	#Welcome to our new Soviet friends !
	option = {
		name = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.15.A
		trigger = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
	}
	#Welcome to our new Soviet friends !
	option = {

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = GER
			}
		}
	}

###########################
# Moscow Berlin Axis
###########################
news_event = {
	id = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.16
	title = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.16.t
	desc = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.16.d
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Hitler_and_Ribbentrop
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#Welcome to our new Comrades
	option = {
		name = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.16.A
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = GER
				original_tag = SOV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = no
					}
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						is_in_faction = yes
					}
				}
				GER = {
					set_faction_name = FACTION_Axis_Powers
					add_to_faction = SOV
				}
			}
			else = {
				GER = {
					create_faction = FACTION_Axis_Powers
					add_to_faction = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SOV
				FRA = {
					has_war_with = GER
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FRA
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SOV
				ENG = {
					has_war_with = GER
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ENG
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SOV
				USA = {
					has_war_with = GER
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = USA
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
	#Wonder how long this ârelationshipâ will last
	option = {
		name = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.16.B
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = GER
					original_tag = SOV
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = Turkey_Promised_To_Soviets
		tag = GER

			GER = {
				OR = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 341
					has_full_control_of_state = 347
					has_full_control_of_state = 340
					has_full_control_of_state = 339
					has_full_control_of_state = 343

							has_full_control_of_state = 341
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 341
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						GER = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 347

					has_full_control_of_state = 1097
					has_full_control_of_state = 211
					has_full_control_of_state = 1098
					has_full_control_of_state = 48
					has_full_control_of_state = 212
					has_full_control_of_state = 1095
					has_full_control_of_state = 1096
				}
			}
			BUL = {
				is_subject_of = GER
				OR = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 1097
					has_full_control_of_state = 211
					has_full_control_of_state = 1098
					has_full_control_of_state = 48
					has_full_control_of_state = 212
					has_full_control_of_state = 1095
					has_full_control_of_state = 1096
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# The treaty is the treaty
	option = {
		name = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.21.A
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = {
				id = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.22
			}
		}
		BUL = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = SOV
				relation = docking_rights
				active = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					country_exists = BUL
				}
			}
			release_puppet = BUL
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.24
	title = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.24.t
	desc = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.24.d
	picture = GFX_report_SOV_Molotov_and_Hitler
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Integrate Romania in the USSR
	option = {
		name = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.24.A
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	# A Loyal independant state
	option = {
		name = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.24.B
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = ROM
			}
		}
		puppet = ROM
		ROM = {
			transfer_state = 41
			transfer_state = 46
			transfer_state = 77
			transfer_state = 834
			transfer_state = 79
			transfer_state = 837
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.25
	title = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.25.t
	desc = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.25.d
	picture = GFX_report_SOV_Molotov_and_Hitler
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = Romania_Promised_To_GER
		tag = SOV
		OR = {
			SOV = {
				OR = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 41
					has_full_control_of_state = 46
					has_full_control_of_state = 77
					has_full_control_of_state = 834
					has_full_control_of_state = 79
					has_full_control_of_state = 837

					has_full_control_of_state = 80
					has_full_control_of_state = 82
					has_full_control_of_state = 84
					has_full_control_of_state = 838
					has_full_control_of_state = 83
					has_full_control_of_state = 76
					has_full_control_of_state = 839
					has_full_control_of_state = 81
				}
			}
			any_country = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
				OR = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 81
					has_full_control_of_state = 41

	id = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.29
	title = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.29.t
	desc = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.29.d
	picture = GFX_report_SOV_Molotov_and_Hitler
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = India_Promised_to_SOV
		tag = GER
		OR = {
			GER = {
				OR = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 895
					has_full_control_of_state = 419
					has_full_control_of_state = 420
					has_full_control_of_state = 421
					has_full_control_of_state = 417
					has_full_control_of_state = 266
					has_full_control_of_state = 413
					has_full_control_of_state = 411
					has_full_control_of_state = 412
					has_full_control_of_state = 416
					has_full_control_of_state = 418
					has_full_control_of_state = 410
					has_full_control_of_state = 414
				}
			}
			any_country = {
				is_subject_of = GER
				OR = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 895
					has_full_control_of_state = 419
					has_full_control_of_state = 420
					has_full_control_of_state = 421
					has_full_control_of_state = 417
					has_full_control_of_state = 266
					has_full_control_of_state = 413
					has_full_control_of_state = 411
					has_full_control_of_state = 412
					has_full_control_of_state = 416
					has_full_control_of_state = 418
					has_full_control_of_state = 410
					has_full_control_of_state = 414
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# The treaty is the treaty
	option = {
		name = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.29.A
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = {
				id = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						GER = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 414
						}
						any_country = {
							is_subject_of = GER
							has_full_control_of_state = 414
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 414
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						GER = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 410
						}
						any_country = {
							is_subject_of = GER
							has_full_control_of_state = 410
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 410
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						GER = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 81
						}
						any_country = {
							is_subject_of = GER
							has_full_control_of_state = 81
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 81
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						GER = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 895
						}
						any_country = {
							is_subject_of = GER
							has_full_control_of_state = 895
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 895
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {

# Iran Joins our Sphere!
###########################
country_event = {
	id = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.30
	title = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.30.t
	desc = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.30.d
	picture = GFX_report_SOV_Molotov_and_Hitler
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Integrate Persia in the USSR
	option = {
		name = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.30.A
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	# A Loyal independant state
	option = {
		name = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.30.B
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = PER
			}
		}
		release_puppet = PER
	}
}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = RAJ
			}
		}
		release_puppet = RAJ
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					country_exists = PAK
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				release_puppet = PAK
				RAJ = {
					annex_country = {
						target = PAK
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Two Loyals independant state
	option = {
		name = GER_Berlin_Moscow_Pact.34.C
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = PAK
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = RAJ
			}
		}
		release_puppet = PAK
		release_puppet = RAJ
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	# We shall join in arms with Germany
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.1.A
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_Tripartite_Pact
		set_temp_variable = {
			GER_Influence_to_add = 5
		}
		add_influence = yes
		YUG = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				GER_Influence_to_add = -5
			}
			add_influence = yes
		}
		ROM = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				GER_Influence_to_add = -5
			}
			add_influence = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						is_in_faction = no
					}
				}
				GER = {
					create_faction = FACTION_Axis_Powers
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			add_to_faction = HUN
		}
		news_event = {
			id = GER_Danube.5
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	# We are strong while independent
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.1.B
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_Tripartite_Pact_Denied
		country_event = {
			days = 1
			id = GER_Danube.32
		}
		GER = {
			create_wargoal = {
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				target = HUN
			}
		}
		news_event = {
			id = GER_Danube.6
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = GER_second_vienna_award_noland
		}
		GER = {

				days = 1
				id = GER_Danube.14
			}
		}
	}
	# We cannot compete ...
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.13.B
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 50
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER

		}

				is_claimed_by = HUN
			}
			remove_claim_by = HUN
		}
	}
}

			target = FROM
		}

			country_event = {
				days = 1
				id = GER_Danube.32
			}
		}
	}
	# Let them fight.

		name = GER_Danube.14.B
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = ROM
				}
				country_event = {
					days = 1
					id = GER_Danube.15
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = HUN
				}
				country_event = {
					days = 1
					id = GER_Danube.16
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = GER_Danube.21.t
	desc = GER_Danube.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_GER_Question_Of_Craiova
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# THIS IS AN OUTRAGE
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.21.A
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				days = 1
				id = GER_Danube.22
			}
		}
	}
	# We really haven't a choice
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.21.B
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROM
				is_claimed_by = BUL
			}
			remove_claim_by = BUL
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				days = 1
				id = GER_Danube.26
			}
		}
	}
}

# GER : FROM refuses our conditions ...
###########################
country_event = {
	id = GER_Danube.22
	title = GER_Danube.22.t
	desc = GER_Danube.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_GER_Question_Of_Craiova
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# What we say goes.
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.22.A
		create_wargoal = {
			type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			target = FROM
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				days = 1
				id = GER_Danube.32
			}
		}
	}
	# Let them fight.
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.22.B
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = ROM
				}
				country_event = {
					days = 1
					id = GER_Danube.23
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = BUL
				}
				country_event = {
					days = 1
					id = GER_Danube.24
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

###########################
# ROM : Germany asks us to keep our oil influx
###########################
country_event = {
	id = GER_Danube.28
	title = GER_Danube.28.t
	desc = GER_Danube.28.d
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Reichstag_on_Fire
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# We Better keep our oil for us ...
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.28.A
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			GER_Influence_to_add = -5
		}
		add_influence = yes
		GER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = GER_ROM_Stoped_Oil_Trade
				target = ROM
			}
		}
	}
	# We really haven't a choice
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.28.B
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			GER_Influence_to_add = 15
		}
		add_influence = yes
		GER = {
			create_import = {
				resource = oil
				amount = 25
				exporter = ROM
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_Trade_With_ROM
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_Trade_With_ROM
					add_idea = GER_Trade_With_ROM_2
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = GER_Trade_With_ROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# ENG : Yugoslavia joins the Tripartite pact !

country_event = {
	id = GER_Danube.29
	title = GER_Danube.29.t
	desc = GER_Danube.29.d
	picture = GFX_report_GER_OKH_Secret_Meeting
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		YUG = {
			is_in_faction_with = GER
		}
		GER = {
			has_government = fascist
		}
		has_start_date < 1941.1.1
	}
	# We have agents on the ground ...
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.29.A
		set_temp_variable = {
			GER_Influence_to_add = -5
		}
		add_influence = yes
		send_equipment = {
			equipment = infantry_equipment
			amount = 500
			target = YUG
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		YUG = {
			country_event = { id = GER_Danube.30 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
}
###########################
# YUG : Coup in the palace !
###########################
country_event = {
	id = GER_Danube.30
	title = GER_Danube.30.t
	desc = GER_Danube.30.d
	picture = GFX_news_YUG_Yugoslav_Coup
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# We have agents on the ground ...
	option = {
		name = GER_Danube.30.A
		retire_country_leader = yes
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = YUG_Dusan_Simovic
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = monarchism
				expire = "1964.1.1"
				traits = {
					POSITION_Prime_Minister
					SUBIDEOLOGY_Monarchism
					L_Old_General
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = YUG_Petar_II_HoG
		leave_faction = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = YUG
			}
			white_peace = YUG
		}
		clr_country_flag = GER_Tripartite_Pact
		set_temp_variable = {
			GER_Influence_to_add = -100
		}
		add_influence = yes
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = huge_decrease
		}
		news_event = { id = GER_Danube.31 hours = 6 }
	}
}

# SOV : Ribbentrop in Moscow
###########################
country_event = {
	id = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.4
	title = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.4.t
	desc = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_GER_Hitler_and_von_Papen
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Nice !
	option = {
		name = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.4.A
		set_global_flag = Molotov_Ribbentrop_Signed
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.5
				days = 1
			}
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = GER
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = GER
				}
				has_government = fascist
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = MR_pact_fascists
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = MR_pact
		}
		GER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = MR_pact
			}
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = befriend
			id = GER
			value = 50
		}
		GER = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = ignore
				id = FIN
				value = 100
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = ignore
				id = EST
				value = 100
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = ignore
				id = LAT
				value = 100
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = ignore
				id = ROM
				value = 50
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = prepare_for_war
				id = SOV
				value = 15
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.5
	title = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.5.t
	desc = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.5.d
	picture = GFX_news_SOV_Molotov_Ribbentrop
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes
	# Germany
	option = {
		name = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.5.A
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
		}
	}
	# Soviet Union
	option = {
		name = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.5.B
		trigger = {
			tag = SOV
		}
	}
	# Allies
	option = {
		name = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.5.C
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = ENG
		}
	}
	# Rest of the world
	option = {
		name = GER_Molotov_Ribbentrop.5.D
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = SOV
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_politician_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		# Abandon the Czechs
		name = GER_Munich_Conference.1.A
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				has_government = communist
				CZE = {
					has_government = communist
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = GER_has_started_war
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = GER
			}
			is_puppet = no			# can't do anything if puppet
		}
		FRA = {
			country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.2
		}
		CZE = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ENG
				modifier = western_betrayal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CZE = {
					is_guaranteed_by = ENG
				}
			}
			ENG = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = CZE
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "CZE"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		# Support the Czechs
		name = GER_Munich_Conference.1.B
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_government = communist
				CZE = {
					has_government = communist
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			remove_from_faction = GER
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			GER = {
				remove_from_faction = ENG
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = condemn_aggression
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE
					generator = {
						69
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CZE = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
			}
			add_to_faction = CZE
		}
		CZE = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "ENG"
				value = 200
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = CZE
					}
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.3
			}
		}
		CZE = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ENG
				modifier = offered_support
			}
		}
	}
}

# FRA: Munich Conference (Britain backed down)
###########################
country_event = {
	id = GER_Munich_Conference.2
	title = GER_Munich_Conference.1.t
	desc = GER_Munich_Conference.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chamberlain_announce
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		# Follow Britain's lead
		name = GER_Munich_Conference.2.A
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = CZE
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				has_government = communist
				CZE = {
					has_government = communist
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = GER_has_started_war
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		CZE = {
			country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.6
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FRA
				modifier = western_betrayal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CZE
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CZE
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CZE = {
					is_guaranteed_by = FRA
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = CZE
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "CZE"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		# Support the Czechs alone
		name = GER_Munich_Conference.2.B
		trigger = {
			is_puppet = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				has_government = communist
				CZE = {
					has_government = communist
				}
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = condemn_aggression
		}
		CZE = {
			country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.5
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FRA
				modifier = offered_support
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.8
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE
					generator = {
						69
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
			}
			ENG = {
				country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.4
				remove_from_faction = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			GER = {
				remove_from_faction = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
				}
				CZE = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
			}
			add_to_faction = CZE
			CZE = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "FRA"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction = no
					is_faction_leader = no
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
				}
				CZE = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
			}
			create_faction = FACTION_Pacte_Oriental
			set_rule = {
				can_create_factions = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = CZE
			CZE = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "FRA"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = GER_Munich_Conference.3
	title = GER_Munich_Conference.1.t
	desc = GER_Munich_Conference.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_czech_soldiers_01
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#Support
	option = {
		name = GER_Munich_Conference.3.A
		trigger = {
			is_puppet = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
				}
			}
			remove_from_faction = FRA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
				}
			}
			ENG = {
				add_to_faction = FRA
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "ENG"
				value = 200
			}
		}

		}

					}

		}

				is_in_faction_with = ENG

			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = GER_has_started_war
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}				#FRA doesn't care if in faction
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CZE = {
					is_guaranteed_by = FRA
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = CZE
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "CZE"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		CZE = {
			country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.44
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FRA
				modifier = western_betrayal
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.7
			effect_tooltip = {

					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE

# CZE: Munich Conference (Czechoslovakia abandoned)

country_event = {
	id = GER_Munich_Conference.6
	title = GER_Munich_Conference.6.t
	desc = GER_Munich_Conference.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_czech_soldiers_01
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		# Surrender the Sudetenland
		name = GER_Munich_Conference.6.A
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				# Decrease chance CZE resists if AUS isn't taken first
				AUS = {
					exists = yes
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				# If they stand a chance they will fight
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio > 0.75
				}
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						NOT = {
							tag = GER
						}
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0				#if you lead a faction, fight
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05				#if you are in a faction, maybe fight
				is_faction_leader = no
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_puppet = yes
				NOT = {
					is_puppet_of = GER
				}				#puppeted CZE wouldn't surrender Sudetenland otherwise
			}
			modifier = {
				# Increase it again if other bordering nations are in Axis
				any_neighbor_country = {
					NOT = {
						tag = GER
					}
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.10
		}
	}
	option = {
		# Refuse anyway
		name = GER_Munich_Conference.6.B
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		GER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = GER_demand_sudetenland_rejected
			}
			set_global_flag = CZE_refused_sudetenland
			country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.9
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						CZE = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
						}
					}
					GER = {
						remove_from_faction = CZE
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE
					generator = {
						69
						74
						1105
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

country_event = {
	id = GER_Munich_Conference.13
	title = GER_Munich_Conference.13.t
	desc = GER_Munich_Conference.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_politician_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		# Agree
		name = GER_Munich_Conference.13.A
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					is_puppet = yes
					GER = {
						AND = {
							has_war_with = ENG
							has_war_with = FRA
						}
					}
					GER = {
						AND = {
							has_war_with = SOV
							OR = {
								has_war_with = ENG
								has_war_with = FRA
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				GER = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_war_with = ENG
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = FRA
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_war_with = FRA
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = ENG
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = GER_Munich_Conference.15
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ENG = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			ENG = {
				add_war_support = 0.1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				add_war_support = 0.1
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
	}
	option = {
		# Refuse
		name = GER_Munich_Conference.13.B
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
				is_puppet = no
				NOT = {
					GER = {
						has_war_with = ENG
						has_war_with = FRA
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					GER = {
						has_war_with = SOV
						OR = {
							has_war_with = ENG
							has_war_with = FRA
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				GER = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_war_with = ENG
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = FRA
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_war_with = FRA
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = ENG
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = GER_Munich_Conference.14
				days = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ENG = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			ENG = {
				add_war_support = 0.1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				add_war_support = 0.1
			}
		}
	}

				}

		}

				}
			}
			add_state_claim = 9
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = CZE
		}
	}
}

				}
			}
			CPU = {
				transfer_state = 73
			}
			HUN = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = CPU
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				1106 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
			CPU = {
				transfer_state = 1106
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				72 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
				POL = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			POL = {
				transfer_state = 72
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				9 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
			BOH = {
				transfer_state = 9
				add_state_core = 9
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				75 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
			BOH = {
				transfer_state = 75
				add_state_core = 75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CZE
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = CZE
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = SLO
				autonomous_state = AUTONOMY_Satellite
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = BOH
				autonomous_state = AUTONOMY_Reichsprotectorate
			}
			else = {
				puppet = SLO
				puppet = BOH
			}
		}
		SLO = {
			add_ideas = {
				SLO_Vojtech_Tuka_HoG
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				hours = 6
				id = GER_Munich_Conference_News.4
			}
			GER = {
				load_oob = GER_BOH
			}
			SLO = {
				load_oob = SLO_independence
			}
			CPU = {
				load_oob = CPU_independence
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = GER_Munich_Conference.17.B
		add_political_power = -40
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CZE
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = CZE
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}

			news_event = {
				hours = 6
				id = GER_Munich_Conference_News.6
			}
		}
	}

		}
	}

		name = GER_Danzig_or_War.1.A

			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = GER_Danzig_or_War.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				annex_country = {
					target = DNZ
					transfer_troops = no
				}
				transfer_state = 798
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = GER_Danzig_or_War.4
				hours = 6
			}
		}
	}
	# Refuse
	option = {
		name = GER_Danzig_or_War.1.B
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio > 0.7
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				any_other_country = {
					is_major = yes
					is_in_faction_with = POL
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = GER_Danzig_or_War.3
				days = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = POL
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = POL
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = POL
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					remove_from_faction = GER
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				hours = 30
				id = GER_Danzig_or_War.5
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = POL
					type = take_state
					generator = {
						798
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			FRA = {
				add_war_support = -0.1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poland Refuses to Cede Danzig
###########################
country_event = {
	id = GER_Danzig_or_War.3	# germany.88
	title = GER_Danzig_or_War.3.t
	desc = GER_Danzig_or_War.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_tanks_02
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = GER_Danzig_or_War.3.A
		declare_war_on = {
			target = POL
			type = take_state
			generator = {
				798
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				DNZ = {
					has_government = fascist
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = DNZ
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		else = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = DNZ
				type = take_state
				generator = {
					85
				}
			}
		}
		add_state_claim = 86
		add_state_claim = 87
		add_state_claim = 98
		add_state_claim = 766
		add_state_claim = 1174
		add_state_claim = 1175
		add_state_claim = 810
		if = {
			limit = {
				ENG = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			ENG = {
				add_war_support = 0.1				#just not cricket
				add_to_faction = POL
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = POL
					enemy = GER
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				add_war_support = 0.1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CZE = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
					has_government = democratic
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			CZE = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = conquer
					id = "GER"
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "POL"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = GER_Danzig_or_War.5	# news.204
	title = GER_Danzig_or_War.5.t
	desc = GER_Danzig_or_War.5.d
	picture = GFX_news_GER_Animated_Invasion_of_Poland
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_for_sender = no
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			sound_effect = "GER_Invasion_of_Poland_Soundeffect"
		}
	}
	#They have ignored every warning!
	option = {
		name = GER_Danzig_or_War.5.A
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction = yes
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = POL
			}
		}
	}
	#
	option = {
		name = GER_Danzig_or_War.5.B
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = GER
		}
	}
	# Together we must stop this aggressor!
	option = {
		name = GER_Danzig_or_War.5.C
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = POL
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = ENG
				enemy = GER
			}
		}
	}
	# This is a grave situation.
	option = {
		name = GER_Danzig_or_War.5.D
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction = no
		}
	}
}

### Flight of Rudolf Hess
# UK Captures Hess
country_event = {
	id = GER_Hess_Flight.1
	title = GER_Hess_Flight.1.t
	desc = GER_Hess_Flight.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_POL_Polish_Forces_Border
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		GER = {
			has_war_with = ENG
		}
		ENG = {
			surrender_progress < 0.01
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = GER_Hess_Flight.1.A
		GER = { 
			country_event = { id = GER_Hess_Flight.2 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# Hitler Notified of Hess' Capture

	id = GER_Hess_Flight.2
	title = GER_Hess_Flight.2.t
	desc = GER_Hess_Flight.2.d
	picture = GFX_news_POL_Polish_Forces_Border

		name = GER_Hess_Flight.2.A

		add_ideas = GER_Martin_Bormann_HoG

			news_event = { id = GER_Hess_Flight.3 }
		}
	}
}
